# 10.7.4 MACsec Registers

@{Key=10.7.4; Title=MACsec Registers; Body=- MACSEC_GCM_KEYTABLE_CONFIG_0
- GCM KeyTable Registers
- Indirect Addressing Access: Register controls for programming the Key tables GCM KeyTable
- Config Register
- Offset: 0x0
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: YT194
- Shadow: N
- Secure: Trust Zone Protected
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0b0xxx,xx00,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxx0,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 UPDATE:
- Key Table Configuration Update control
- SW has to trigger by writing Logic 1 to the UPDATE field after
programming DATA and other config fields. Poll for the value to become Logic0 to ensure the operation is complete. 0 = DONE :Update operation is done or No update operation is initiated 1 = START :Start the Update operation 0x0 CTLR_SEL:
- MACSEC Controller selection (Transmit or Receive)
0 = TX :MACSEC Transmitter 1 = RX :MACSEC Receiver 0x0 RW:
- Key Table access direction
0 = READ :Read entries from GCM KeyTable 1 = WRITE :Write to GCM KeyTable 4:0 0x0 TABLE_INDEX:
- Key Table slot Address or Index where the Key would be written
- MACSEC_GCM_KEYTABLE_DATA_0
The following register set holds the data value for KeyTable.Format of the data resembles exactly the KeyTable format. This is an array of 13 identical register entries; the register fields below apply to each entry. Full register list is: MACSEC_GCM_KEYTABLE_DATA_<i>, among which <i> belongs to <0..12>.
- Offset: 0x4,..,0x34

- MACsec Registers
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- Secure: Trust Zone Protected
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0b0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
31:0 0x0
- DATA
- MACSEC_MAC_CONTROL_0
- Adding register bits to control CRC mask bits for MAC
The lock bit is used as a mask for the register field which is being protected. In order to change the configuration of the register bit, the lock bit should be disabled until the required functionality is complete. Programming the lock bit to 1 will override the register fields with the secure value (i.e., in case of DCRCC, CRC will be checked for all packets)
- Offset: 0x4c
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- Secure: Trust Zone Protected
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000007 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,x111)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x1 RXQ_RSF_LOCK:
- Set to 0 to configure
- EQOS_MTL_Q[n]_MTL_RXQ[n]_OPERATION_MODE_0.RSF n={0..7} for
- EQOS
- Set to 0 to configure
- MGBE_DWCXG_MTL_TCQ[n]_MTL_RXQ[n]_OPERATION_MODE_0.RSF
n={0..9} for MGBE 0x1 RXQ_FEP_LOCK:
- Set to 0 to configure
- EQOS_MTL_Q[n]_MTL_RXQ[n]_OPERATION_MODE_0.FEP n={0..7} for
- EQOS
- Set to 0 to configure
- MGBE_DWCXG_MTL_TCQ[n]_MTL_RXQ[n]_OPERATION_MODE_0.FEF
n={0..9} for MGBE 0x1 DCRCC_LOCK:
- Set to 0 to configure EQOS_MAC_MAC_EXT_CONFIGURATION_0.DCRCC
for EQOS
- Set to 0 to configure
- MGBE_DWCXG_CORE_MAC_RX_CONFIGURATION_0.DCRCC for MGBE

- MACsec Registers
- MACSEC_RX_ICV_ERROR_CONTROL_0
- MACSEC Ingress ICV failures Threshold register
- Offset: 0x4000
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00003fff (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,0011,1111,1111,1111)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
15:0 0x3fff ICV_ERROR_THRESHOLD:
- When Threshold count is reached, MACSEC sets ICV Error event and
generates an interrupt if interrupt is enabled.
- Setting "0" means no reporting of ICV Errors. Should program with
Non zero value to get the ICV Error interrupt.
- MACSEC_INTERRUPT_COMMON_STATUS_0
- MACSEC Common (TX and RX controller) Interrupt Status Register
This status register will have a status bit that is OR(All MACSEC TX interrupts). Similarly a status bit for OR(All MACSEC RX Interrupts). This will help to quickly identify the source of interrupt whether it is MACSEC TX or MACSEC RX controller.
- Offset: 0x4004
- Read/Write: RO
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,x000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 MSEC_SFTY_ERR_INTR:
- MACSEC Safety Interrupt status
0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 MSEC_RX_INTR:
- MACSEC RX controller Interrupt status
0 = UNSET 1 = SET

- MACsec Registers
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 MSEC_TX_INTR:
- MACSEC TX controller Interrupt status
0 = UNSET 1 = SET
- MACSEC_TX_INTERRUPT_MASK_0
- MACSEC Egress Interrupt Mask Register
- Offset: 0x4008
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,x0xx,0000,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xx00)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 DBG_BUF_CAPTURE_DONE_INT_EN:
- Interrupt enable for Tx Debug Buffer capture done event
0 = DISABLE :Masks the Interrupt generation 1 = ENABLE :Enables the Interrupt generation 0x0 MTU_CHECK_FAIL_INT_EN:
- Interrupt enable for MTU Check fail
0 = DISABLE :Masks the Interrupt generation 1 = ENABLE :Enables the Interrupt generation 0x0 AES_GCM_BUF_OVF_INT_EN:
- AES_GCM_BUF overflow to trigger the Interrupt. Buffer overflow event
should not get triggered during normal course of operation. 0 = DISABLE :Masks the Interrupt generation 1 = ENABLE :Enables the Interrupt generation 0x0 SC_AN_NOT_VALID_INT_EN:
- Interrupt for invalid AN state of an SC. This state is reached when
the incoming packet from MAC to MACSEC maps to an SC where the current AN is not enabled or re-initialized 0 = DISABLE :Masks the Interrupt generation 1 = ENABLE :Enables the Interrupt generation 0x0 MAC_CRC_ERROR_INT_EN:
- Interrupt if CRC error is detected in the incoming frame from MAC to
- MACSEC
0 = DISABLE :Masks the Interrupt generation 1 = ENABLE :Enables the Interrupt generation

- MACsec Registers
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 PN_EXHAUSTED_INT_EN:
- Interrupt if Packet Number of SA/AN is exhausted
0 = DISABLE :Masks the Interrupt generation 1 = ENABLE :Enables the Interrupt generation 0x0 PN_THRSHLD_RCHD_INT_EN:
- Interrupt if Threshold value of Packet Number of SA/AN is reached
to indicate the next AN should be programmed and available before PN gets fully exhausted 0 = DISABLE :Masks the Interrupt generation 1 = ENABLE :Enables the Interrupt generation
- MACSEC_TX_INTERRUPT_STATUS_0
- MACSEC Egress Interrupt Status Register
Status bits corresponding to an Interrupt event Status bits are sticky. They get cleared when written with 1
- Offset: 0x400c
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,x0xx,0000,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xx00)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 DBG_BUF_CAPTURE_DONE:
- Tx Debug Buffer capture is done
0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 MTU_CHECK_FAIL:
- MTU Check failed. The Incoming packet (from MAC to MACSEC) length is
greater than programmed MTU Length 0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 AES_GCM_BUF_OVF:
- AES_GCM_BUF overflow occurred. Buffer overflow event should not get
triggered during normal course of operation. 0 = UNSET 1 = SET

- MACsec Registers
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 SC_AN_NOT_VALID:
- Invalid AN state of an SC. This state is reached when the incoming packet
from MAC to MACSEC maps to an SC where the current AN is not enabled or re-initialized 0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 MAC_CRC_ERROR:
- CRC error is detected in the incoming frame from MAC to MACSEC
0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 PN_EXHAUSTED:
- Packet Number of SA/AN is exhausted
0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 PN_THRSHLD_RCHD:
- Threshold value of Packet Number of SA/AN is reached
to indicate the next AN should be programmed and available before PN gets fully exhausted 0 = UNSET 1 = SET
- MACSEC_TX_INTERRUPT_SET_0
- MACSEC Egress Interrupt Set Register
This is a write-only register which can be used to set the interrupt status bit. A write to this register causes the bits in TX_INTERRUPT_STATUS register to be set if the corresponding bit in write data is 1'b1. Read always returns 'h0.
- Offset: 0x4010
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,x0xx,0000,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xx00)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 DBG_BUF_CAPTURE_DONE:
- Tx Debug Buffer capture is done
0 = UNSET 1 = SET

- MACsec Registers
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 MTU_CHECK_FAIL:
- MTU Check failed. The Incoming packet (MAC to MACSEC) length is
greater than programmed MTU Length 0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 AES_GCM_BUF_OVF:
- AES_GCM_BUF overflow occurred. Buffer overflow event should not get
triggered during normal course of operation. 0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 SC_AN_NOT_VALID:
- Invalid AN state of an SC. This state is reached when the incoming packet
(from MAC to MACSEC) maps to an SC where the current AN is not enabled or re-initialized 0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 MAC_CRC_ERROR:
- CRC error is detected in the incoming frame from MAC to MACSEC
0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 PN_EXHAUSTED:
- Packet Number of SA/AN is exhausted
0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 PN_THRSHLD_RCHD:
- Threshold value of Packet Number of SA/AN is reached
to indicate the next AN should be programmed and available before PN gets fully exhausted 0 = UNSET 1 = SET
- MACSEC_TX_SC_PN_THRESHOLD_STATUS0_0
Following registers indicate the SCs and ANs for which PN Threshold is Reached. PN Threshold status should be used by the SW to identify the future ANs and the associated keys to be programmed to avoid reaching invalid AN state. SW should enable the future ANs and keys and clear this bit. If SW has already programmed the future ANs it can just clear the status. Writing "1'b1" to a bit clears it.
- Offset: 0x4018
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y

- MACsec Registers
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0b0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description

- SCn_AN[bit1] = 1, AN01 reached threshold
- SCn_AN[bit2] = 1, AN10 reached threshold
- SCn_AN[bit3] = 1, AN11 reached threshold

- MACSEC_TX_SC_ERROR_INTERRUPT_STATUS_0

- MACsec Registers
Following register indicates the SCs that got into Error state due to various events like Invalid AN (means SC has reached a state where the new AN is not available). Invalid AN state is reached typically becuse SW has not enabled the new AN in advance and previous AN is exhuasted (i.e. PN Max has reached and new packet has come).
- Offset: 0x402c
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,0000,0000,0000,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
15:0 0x0
- SC_AN_NOT_AVAILABLE
- MACSEC_RX_INTERRUPT_MASK_0
- MACSEC Ingress Interrupt Mask Register
- Offset: 0x4048
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,x000,00x0,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xx0x)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 DBG_BUF_CAPTURE_DONE_INT_EN:
- Interrupt enable for Rx Debug Buffer capture done event
0 = DISABLE :Masks the Interrupt generation 1 = ENABLE :Enables the Interrupt generation 0x0 ICV_ERROR_INT_EN:
- Interrupt enable for ICV failures threshold
0 = DISABLE :Masks the Interrupt generation 1 = ENABLE :Enables the Interrupt generation 0x0 REPLAY_ERROR_INT_EN:
- Interrupt enable for Replay Check fail
0 = DISABLE :Masks the Interrupt generation 1 = ENABLE :Enables the Interrupt generation 0x0 MTU_CHECK_FAIL_INT_EN:
- Interrupt enable for MTU Check fail
0 = DISABLE :Masks the Interrupt generation 1 = ENABLE :Enables the Interrupt generation

- MACsec Registers
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 AES_GCM_BUF_OVF_INT_EN:
- AES_GCM_BUF overflow to trigger the Interrupt. Buffer overflow event
should not get triggered during normal course of operation. 0 = DISABLE :Masks the Interrupt generation 1 = ENABLE :Enables the Interrupt generation 0x0 MAC_CRC_ERROR_INT_EN:
- Interrupt if CRC error is detected in the incoming frame from LINE side
- Module to MACSEC
0 = DISABLE :Masks the Interrupt generation 1 = ENABLE :Enables the Interrupt generation 0x0 PN_EXHAUSTED_INT_EN:
- Interrupt if Packet Number of SA/AN is exhausted
0 = DISABLE :Masks the Interrupt generation 1 = ENABLE :Enables the Interrupt generation
- MACSEC_RX_INTERRUPT_STATUS_0
- MACSEC Ingress Interrupt Status Register
Status bits corresponding to an Interrupt event Status bits are sticky. They get cleared when written with 1
- Offset: 0x404c
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,x000,00x0,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xx0x)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 DBG_BUF_CAPTURE_DONE:
- Rx Debug Buffer capture is done
0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 ICV_ERROR:
- ICV failures Threshold count is reached
0 = UNSET 1 = SET

- MACsec Registers
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 REPLAY_ERROR: Replay Protection Check failed.
- The PN of just received frame is smaller than PN of last received frame or
outside allowed window. 0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 MTU_CHECK_FAIL:
- MTU Check failed. The Incoming packet (from LINE side module to
- MACSEC) length is greater than programmed MTU Length
0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 AES_GCM_BUF_OVF:
- AES_GCM_BUF overflow occurred. Buffer overflow event should not get
triggered during normal course of operation. 0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 MAC_CRC_ERROR:
- CRC error is detected in the incoming frame (from LINE side module to
- MACSEC)
0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 PN_EXHAUSTED:
- Packet Number of SA/AN is exhausted
0 = UNSET 1 = SET
- MACSEC_RX_INTERRUPT_SET_0
- MACSEC Ingress Interrupt Set Register
This is a write-only register which can be used to set the interrupt status bit. A write to this register causes the bits in RX_INTERRUPT_STATUS register to be set if the corresponding bit in write data is 1'b1. Read always returns 'h0.
- Offset: 0x4050
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,x000,00x0,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xx0x)

- MACsec Registers

- Reset

- ICV failures Threshold count is reached
0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 REPLAY_ERROR: Replay Protection Check failed.

outside allowed window. 0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 MTU_CHECK_FAIL:

- MACSEC_STATS_CONTROL_0
- MACSEC TX Statistics Counters

- MACsec Registers
- Offset: 0x900c
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 RD_CPY:
- Control bit to read counter values from the copy
0 = DISABLE :Read from raw counters 1 = ENABLE :read from copied set 0x0 TK_CPY: take a copy of counters current values
- The bit is auto-cleared to zero once the copy is done
0 = DONE 1 = START 0x0 CNT_RL_OVR:
- Counters roll over control bit
0 = DISABLE :Counters do NOT roll over to zero after reaching the maximum value 1 = ENABLE :Counters roll over to zero after reaching the maximum value 0x0 CNT_CLR: Resets the statistics counters to zero.
- The bit is auto-cleared to zero once the counters are reset to zero
0 = DONE 1 = START

- Description
31:0 0x0 RXPKTSOKHI:
- INPKTS_OK STAT Counter Data Upper 32-bits
- MACSEC_TX_INPKTS_CRCIN_NOTVALID_LO_0
- TX Incoming Packets CRC NotVALID Counter
- This counter counts the number of received packets that failed the CRC check These are the
packets that come from system side MAC in Egress direction Lower 32-bit of CRC check failed packets count
- Offset: 0x9260
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0b0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
31:0 0x0 CRCNVLDLO:
- Egress INPKTS_CRC_NOTVALID Counter, Lower 32-bits
- MACSEC_TX_INPKTS_CRCIN_NOTVALID_HI_0
- Upper 32-bit of TX Inpackets CRC failed count
- Offset: 0x9264
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0

- Reset
- Description

- Egress INPKTS_CRC_NOTVALID Counter, Upper 32-bits

- MACsec Registers
- MACSEC_RX_INPKTS_CRCIN_NOTVALID_LO_0
- RX Incoming Packets CRC NotVALID Counter
- This counter counts the number of received packets that failed the CRC check These are the
packets that come from line side in Ingress direction Lower 32-bit of CRC check failed packets count.

- Description
31:0 0x0 CRCNVLDHI:
- Ingress INPKTS_CRC_NOTVALID Counter, Upper 32-bits
- MACSEC_CONTROL0_0
- MACSEC Control Register 0
- Offset: 0xd000
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: N

- MACsec Registers
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00500000 (0bxxxx,xxx0,0101,0xx0,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,0xx0)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 TX_LKP_MISS_NON_SECURE_INTR:
- When TX look up miss event occurs, hw will assert secure/non-secure
intr based on this bit. Reset_Domain: Secure_Reset. 0 = SECURE_INTR 1 = NON_SECURE_INTR 0x0 RX_LKP_MISS_NON_SECURE_INTR:
- When RX look up miss event occurs, hw will assert secure/non-secure
intr based on this bit. Reset_Domain: Secure_Reset. 0 = SECURE_INTR 1 = NON_SECURE_INTR 22:21 0x2 VALIDATE_FRAMES:
- MACSEC Receive Frame Validate control
Reset_Domain: Secure_Reset. 0 = DISABLED :ICV check is disabled. SecTag and ICV fields are removed from the frame before forwarding it to the next module 1 = CHECK :ICV check is done. And the InPktsInValid counter is updated based on ICV check result. 2 = STRICT :ICV check is done. If ICV check fails, the frame is dropped (CRC of the frame is corrupted) and InPktsNotValid counter is updated. 0x1 RX_REPLAY_PROT_EN:
- MACSEC Receive Frame Replay Protection enable control
Reset_Domain: Secure_Reset. 0 = DISABLE :Disable Replay Protection 1 = ENABLE :Enable Replay Protection 0x0 RX_LOOKUP_MISS:
- MACSEC Receive: Select an action for Bypass LookUP tables miss (No
matching entry found in the Bypass LUT). This bit is applicable only for
- Bypass LuT and not SC index LuT
Reset_Domain: Secure_Reset. 0 = DROP :Corrupt the packet on bypass tables lookup miss 1 = BYPASS :Bypass the packet on bypass tables lookup miss 0x0 RX_ENB:
- MACSEC Receive Controller enable bit. Bypasses the MACSEC RX
controller Reset_Domain: Secure_Reset. 0 = DISABLE :Bypasses MACSEC Receive Controller 1 = ENABLE :Enables MACSEC Receive Controller 0x0 TX_LOOKUP_MISS:
- MACSEC Transmit: Select an action for LookUP tables miss (No
matching entry found in both Bypass and SC-Index LUTs). Reset_Domain: Secure_Reset. 0 = DROP :Corrupt the packet on tables lookup miss 1 = BYPASS :Bypass the packet on tables lookup miss

- MACsec Registers
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 TX_ENB:
- MACSEC Transmit Controller enable bit. Bypasses the MACSEC TX
controller Reset_Domain: Secure_Reset. 0 = DISABLE :Disables MACSEC Transmit Controller 1 = ENABLE :Enables MACSEC Transmit Controller
- MACSEC_LUT_CONFIG_0
- Indirect Addressing access: Register controls for programming the LookUP tables
- Offset: 0xd004
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0b0xxx,xx00,xxxx,x000,xxxx,xxxx,xxx0,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 UPDATE:
- LookUP Table Configuration Update control
- SW has to trigger by writing Logic 1 to the UPDATE field after
programming DATA and other config fields.
- Poll for the value to become Logic0 to ensure the operation is
complete. 0 = DONE :Update operation is done or No update operation is initiated 1 = START :Start the Update operation 0x0 CTLR_SEL:
- MACSEC Controller selection (Transmit or Receiver)
0 = TX :MACSEC Transmitter 1 = RX :MACSEC Receiver 0x0 RW:
- Table access direction
0 = READ :Read entries from LookUP Table 1 = WRITE :Write to LookUP Table 18:16 0x0 LUT_SEL:
- LookUP table Selection control
0 = BYPASS 1 = SC_INDX 2 = SC_PARAM 3 = SC_STATE 4 = SA_STATE 4:0 0x0 TABLE_ENTRY_INDEX:
- Table slot Address or Index where an entry would be written

- MACsec Registers
- MACSEC_LUT_DATA_0
- MACSEC LUT Data register
Following register-set holds the data value for a LookUP table. Format of the data resembles the exact table that is to be programmed. This is an array of 7 identical register entries; the register fields below apply to each entry. Full register list is: MACSEC_LUT_DATA_<i>, among which <i> belongs to <0..6>.

- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0

- MACSEC_INTERRUPT_SET0_0
This is a write-only register which can be used to set the interrupt status bit. A write to this register causes the bits in INTERRUPT_STATUS0 register to be set if the corresponding bit in write data is 1'b1. Read always returns 'h0.

- MACSEC_CONTROL1_0
- MACSEC Control Register 1
- Offset: 0xe000
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0b0xxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxx0,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,x0x0)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 INT_LPBK_MODE:
- Internal Loopback mode. When this bit is set to ENABLE, MACSEC TX output
lines will be connectd to MACSEC RX input lines internally. It takes 1us for this bit to take effect inside the MACSEC logic. This bit is also used as the loopback
- FIFO flush bit and needs to be deasserted for 2us for the flush operation to
complete. 0 = DISABLE :Disable Loopback 1 = ENABLE :Enable Loopback 0x0 RX_MTU_CHECK_ENB:
- MACSEC Receive Maximum Transmission Unit Check Control bit
0 = DISABLE :Disable MTU check 1 = ENABLE :Enable MTU check 0x0 TX_LUT_PRIORITY:
- MACSEC Transmit SC and Bypass LUTs priority Control
0 = SC :SC Index LUT has the priority over Bypass LUT 1 = BYPASS :Bypass LUT has the priority over SC-Index LUT 0x0 TX_MTU_CHECK_ENB:
- MACSEC Transmit Maximum Transmission Unit Check Control bit
0 = DISABLE :Disable MTU check 1 = ENABLE :Enable MTU check

- MACsec Registers
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
31:16 0x8e NUM_ERR:
- Number of errors connected to this collator. This is passed as a build
time option to the plugin 5:0 0x5 NUM_ERR_SLICES:
- Number of error slices supported by this error collator, does not
include the GlobalSpace and is derived by ceil (NUM_ERR/32). SW shall first read this register to determine the number of slices and read the required number of Error_Status registers .
- MACSEC_ERRCOLLATOR_SWRESET_0
- Offset: 0xf004
- Read/Write: WO
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxx0)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 SWRST: 1'b1 : Issue a SW reset to the Error Collator. This will reset all the registers(Except SCR), counters and logic of the Error Collator. SW can use this bit to flush errors logged into the error collator for ex, after Boot, SC7/8 exit. 1'b0 : Do nothing, reset value. This bit is auto-cleared.
- MACSEC_ERRCOLLATOR_MISSIONERR_TYPE_0
- Offset: 0xf008
- Read/Write: RO
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000005 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xx00,0101)

- MACsec Registers
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
5:0 0x5 CODE:
- This register indicates the fault code of the error line based on the value
of MISSIONERR_INDEX Register.
- This can be used by a fault handling agent to triage an error without
requiring device-specific code.The possible values of this field are: 6'd0 : None 6'd1 : Parity Error on internal data path 6'd2 : ECC SEC Error on internal data path 6'd3 : ECC DED Error on internal data path 6'd4 : Comparator Error 6'd5 : Register Parity Error 6'd6 : Parity Error from on-chip SRAM/Fifo 6'd7 : ECC SEC Error from on-chip SRAM/Fifo 6'd8 : ECC DED Error from on-chip SRAM/Fifo 6'd9 : Clock Monitor Error 6'd10 : Voltage Error 6'd11 : Temperature Error 6'd12 : CRC Error on internal data path 6'd16 : SW Corrected Error 6'd17 : SW Uncorrected Error 6'd18 : SW Generic Error 6'd20 : ECC SED Error on internal data path 6'd21 : ECC SED Error from on-chip SRAM/Fifo 6'd32 : Other HW Corrected Error 6'd33 : Other HW Uncorrected Error
- All other values : Reserved
- MACSEC_ERRCOLLATOR_CURRENT_COUNTER_VALUE_0
- Offset: 0xf00c
- Read/Write: RO
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxx0,0000,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
8:0 0x0 VALUE:
- Provides the current value of the counter corresponding to the error in
MissionErr_Index Register. Default provides the value of error 0 counter.
- Bit[8] is the ovrerflow bit post which the counter saturates and does not
counter further.
- MACSEC_ERRCOLLATOR_MISSIONERR_USERVALUE_0
- Offset: 0xf010
- Read/Write: RO
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N

- MACsec Registers
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0xdead0000 (0b1101,1110,1010,1101,0000,0000,0000,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
31:0 0xdead0000 VALUE:
- Reflects the value on the error_<i>_user when error_<i>_pulse =
MissionError.
- Only the user signals corresponding to the first error_<i>_pulse
only will b elatched.Subsequent values will be dropped.
- The signals will get latched only when
ERRSLICE<n>_MISSIONERR_STATUS is CLEAR. IPs must tie off the unused bits of this signals to 0, if unused.
- MACSEC_ERRCOLLATOR_MISSIONERR_INDEX_0
- Offset: 0xf014
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,0000,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
7:0 0x0 IDX:
- BINARY Encoded. For error number 32, register should be programmed
with value 0x20. Write to this register with Error number will update:
- MISSIONERR_TYPE Register with the Error-Code for the Error.
- CURRENT_COUNTER_VALUE Register with the error's SEC/DED Counter.
- MISSIONERR_USERVALUE with value of the first error_<i>_user signal.
SW can use this to trage the error. number shall update the MISSIONERR_TYPE register with the error code and the Current_Counter_Value register with the value of the errors SEC/DED counter. SW can use this register to triage the error.
- MACSEC_ERRCOLLATOR_CORRECTABLE_THRESHOLD_0
- Offset: 0xf018
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,0000,0000)

- MACsec Registers
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
7:0 0x0 COUNT:
- Threshold value for all SEC Fault Reporting Units connected to this error
collator.
- SEC Errors are logged once the threshold is reached and the overflow bit
is set. 7'b0 : Log SEC error after receiving 1 Error. 7'b1 : Log SEC error after receiving 2 Errors. ... 7'bFF : Log SEC error after receiving 256 Errors.
- MACSEC_ERRCOLLATOR_MISSIONERR_INJECT_UNLOCK_0
- Offset: 0xf01c
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,0000,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
7:0 0x0 VALUE:
- Writes to ERRSLICE_XXX_MISSIONERR_INJECT registers are disabled until
this register is written with a value of 0xE1.
- This is to prevent an inadvertent safety error injection in the safety plugin
due to: 1. A fault on ERRSLICE_XXX_MISSIONERR_INJECT register itself. 2. Erroneous SW.
- The register shall be written with a value of 0x0 to reestablish the lock after
user has completed the error injection testing. 0xE1 : Unlock the MISSIONERR_INJECT Register 0x0 : Lock the MISSIONERR_INJECT Register 0 = LOCK 225 = UNLOCK

- MACsec Registers
- MACSEC_ERRCOLLATOR_ERRSLICE0_LATENTERR_STATUS_0
SW must write 1 to clear the fields of this register. Bits in this register continue to be logged independent of the value of LatentError_Enable register, to avoid silent dropping of errors.

- Read/Write: R/W

- MACSEC_ERRCOLLATOR_ERRSLICE1_MISSIONERR_STATUS_0
SW must write 1 to clear the fields of this register.

- MACsec Registers
Bits in this register continue to be logged independent of the value of MissionError_Enable register, to avoid silent dropping of errors.

- MACSEC_ERRCOLLATOR_ERRSLICE1_LATENTERR_STATUS_0
SW must write 1 to clear the fields of this register.

- MACsec Registers
Bits in this register continue to be logged independent of the value of LatentError_Enable register, to avoid silent dropping of errors.

- MACSEC_ERRCOLLATOR_ERRSLICE2_LATENTERR_STATUS_0
SW must write 1 to clear the fields of this register. Bits in this register continue to be logged independent of the value of LatentError_Enable register, to avoid silent dropping of errors.

## 10.8 10G Ethernet Controller}(@{Key=10.7.4; Title=MACsec Registers; Body=- MACSEC_GCM_KEYTABLE_CONFIG_0
- GCM KeyTable Registers
- Indirect Addressing Access: Register controls for programming the Key tables GCM KeyTable
- Config Register
- Offset: 0x0
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: YT194
- Shadow: N
- Secure: Trust Zone Protected
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0b0xxx,xx00,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxx0,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 UPDATE:
- Key Table Configuration Update control
- SW has to trigger by writing Logic 1 to the UPDATE field after
programming DATA and other config fields. Poll for the value to become Logic0 to ensure the operation is complete. 0 = DONE :Update operation is done or No update operation is initiated 1 = START :Start the Update operation 0x0 CTLR_SEL:
- MACSEC Controller selection (Transmit or Receive)
0 = TX :MACSEC Transmitter 1 = RX :MACSEC Receiver 0x0 RW:
- Key Table access direction
0 = READ :Read entries from GCM KeyTable 1 = WRITE :Write to GCM KeyTable 4:0 0x0 TABLE_INDEX:
- Key Table slot Address or Index where the Key would be written
- MACSEC_GCM_KEYTABLE_DATA_0
The following register set holds the data value for KeyTable.Format of the data resembles exactly the KeyTable format. This is an array of 13 identical register entries; the register fields below apply to each entry. Full register list is: MACSEC_GCM_KEYTABLE_DATA_<i>, among which <i> belongs to <0..12>.
- Offset: 0x4,..,0x34

- MACsec Registers
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- Secure: Trust Zone Protected
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0b0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
31:0 0x0
- DATA
- MACSEC_MAC_CONTROL_0
- Adding register bits to control CRC mask bits for MAC
The lock bit is used as a mask for the register field which is being protected. In order to change the configuration of the register bit, the lock bit should be disabled until the required functionality is complete. Programming the lock bit to 1 will override the register fields with the secure value (i.e., in case of DCRCC, CRC will be checked for all packets)

- Read/Write: R/W

- EQOS

- MACsec Registers
- MACSEC_RX_ICV_ERROR_CONTROL_0
- MACSEC Ingress ICV failures Threshold register
- Offset: 0x4000
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00003fff (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,0011,1111,1111,1111)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
15:0 0x3fff ICV_ERROR_THRESHOLD:
- When Threshold count is reached, MACSEC sets ICV Error event and
generates an interrupt if interrupt is enabled.
- Setting "0" means no reporting of ICV Errors. Should program with
Non zero value to get the ICV Error interrupt.
- MACSEC_INTERRUPT_COMMON_STATUS_0
- MACSEC Common (TX and RX controller) Interrupt Status Register
This status register will have a status bit that is OR(All MACSEC TX interrupts). Similarly a status bit for OR(All MACSEC RX Interrupts). This will help to quickly identify the source of interrupt whether it is MACSEC TX or MACSEC RX controller.
- Offset: 0x4004
- Read/Write: RO

- Shadow: N

0 = UNSET 1 = SET

- MACSEC

- MACSEC_TX_INTERRUPT_SET_0
- MACSEC Egress Interrupt Set Register
This is a write-only register which can be used to set the interrupt status bit. A write to this register causes the bits in TX_INTERRUPT_STATUS register to be set if the corresponding bit in write data is 1'b1. Read always returns 'h0.

- MACSEC_TX_SC_PN_THRESHOLD_STATUS0_0
Following registers indicate the SCs and ANs for which PN Threshold is Reached. PN Threshold status should be used by the SW to identify the future ANs and the associated keys to be programmed to avoid reaching invalid AN state. SW should enable the future ANs and keys and clear this bit. If SW has already programmed the future ANs it can just clear the status. Writing "1'b1" to a bit clears it.
- Offset: 0x4018
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y

- MACSEC_TX_SC_ERROR_INTERRUPT_STATUS_0

- MACsec Registers
Following register indicates the SCs that got into Error state due to various events like Invalid AN (means SC has reached a state where the new AN is not available). Invalid AN state is reached typically becuse SW has not enabled the new AN in advance and previous AN is exhuasted (i.e. PN Max has reached and new packet has come).
- Offset: 0x402c
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,0000,0000,0000,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
15:0 0x0
- SC_AN_NOT_AVAILABLE
- MACSEC_RX_INTERRUPT_MASK_0
- MACSEC Ingress Interrupt Mask Register
- Offset: 0x4048
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,x000,00x0,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xx0x)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 DBG_BUF_CAPTURE_DONE_INT_EN:
- Interrupt enable for Rx Debug Buffer capture done event
0 = DISABLE :Masks the Interrupt generation 1 = ENABLE :Enables the Interrupt generation 0x0 ICV_ERROR_INT_EN:
- Interrupt enable for ICV failures threshold
0 = DISABLE :Masks the Interrupt generation 1 = ENABLE :Enables the Interrupt generation 0x0 REPLAY_ERROR_INT_EN:
- Interrupt enable for Replay Check fail
0 = DISABLE :Masks the Interrupt generation 1 = ENABLE :Enables the Interrupt generation 0x0 MTU_CHECK_FAIL_INT_EN:
- Interrupt enable for MTU Check fail
0 = DISABLE :Masks the Interrupt generation 1 = ENABLE :Enables the Interrupt generation

- MACsec Registers
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 AES_GCM_BUF_OVF_INT_EN:
- AES_GCM_BUF overflow to trigger the Interrupt. Buffer overflow event
should not get triggered during normal course of operation. 0 = DISABLE :Masks the Interrupt generation 1 = ENABLE :Enables the Interrupt generation 0x0 MAC_CRC_ERROR_INT_EN:
- Interrupt if CRC error is detected in the incoming frame from LINE side
- Module to MACSEC
0 = DISABLE :Masks the Interrupt generation 1 = ENABLE :Enables the Interrupt generation 0x0 PN_EXHAUSTED_INT_EN:
- Interrupt if Packet Number of SA/AN is exhausted
0 = DISABLE :Masks the Interrupt generation 1 = ENABLE :Enables the Interrupt generation
- MACSEC_RX_INTERRUPT_STATUS_0
- MACSEC Ingress Interrupt Status Register
Status bits corresponding to an Interrupt event Status bits are sticky. They get cleared when written with 1
- Offset: 0x404c
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,x000,00x0,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xx0x)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 DBG_BUF_CAPTURE_DONE:
- Rx Debug Buffer capture is done
0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 ICV_ERROR:
- ICV failures Threshold count is reached
0 = UNSET 1 = SET

- MACsec Registers
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 REPLAY_ERROR: Replay Protection Check failed.
- The PN of just received frame is smaller than PN of last received frame or
outside allowed window. 0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 MTU_CHECK_FAIL:
- MTU Check failed. The Incoming packet (from LINE side module to
- MACSEC) length is greater than programmed MTU Length
0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 AES_GCM_BUF_OVF:
- AES_GCM_BUF overflow occurred. Buffer overflow event should not get
triggered during normal course of operation. 0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 MAC_CRC_ERROR:
- CRC error is detected in the incoming frame (from LINE side module to
- MACSEC)
0 = UNSET 1 = SET 0x0 PN_EXHAUSTED:
- Packet Number of SA/AN is exhausted
0 = UNSET 1 = SET
- MACSEC_RX_INTERRUPT_SET_0
- MACSEC Ingress Interrupt Set Register
This is a write-only register which can be used to set the interrupt status bit. A write to this register causes the bits in RX_INTERRUPT_STATUS register to be set if the corresponding bit in write data is 1'b1. Read always returns 'h0.
- Offset: 0x4050
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N

- MACSEC TX Statistics Counters

- MACsec Registers
- Offset: 0x900c
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 RD_CPY:
- Control bit to read counter values from the copy
0 = DISABLE :Read from raw counters 1 = ENABLE :read from copied set 0x0 TK_CPY: take a copy of counters current values
- The bit is auto-cleared to zero once the copy is done
0 = DONE 1 = START 0x0 CNT_RL_OVR:
- Counters roll over control bit
0 = DISABLE :Counters do NOT roll over to zero after reaching the maximum value 1 = ENABLE :Counters roll over to zero after reaching the maximum value 0x0 CNT_CLR: Resets the statistics counters to zero.
- The bit is auto-cleared to zero once the counters are reset to zero
0 = DONE 1 = START
- MACSEC_TX_PKTS_UNTG_LO_0
- TX OutPackets UnTagged Counter
- Offset: 0x9010
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0b0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
31:0 0x0 TXPKTSUTLO:
- OUTPKTS_UNTAGGED STAT Counter Data Lower 32-bits

- MACsec Registers

31:0 0x0 CRCNVLDHI:
- Ingress INPKTS_CRC_NOTVALID Counter, Upper 32-bits
- MACSEC_CONTROL0_0
- MACSEC Control Register 0
- Offset: 0xd000
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: N

- MACsec Registers
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00500000 (0bxxxx,xxx0,0101,0xx0,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,0xx0)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 TX_LKP_MISS_NON_SECURE_INTR:
- When TX look up miss event occurs, hw will assert secure/non-secure
intr based on this bit. Reset_Domain: Secure_Reset. 0 = SECURE_INTR 1 = NON_SECURE_INTR 0x0 RX_LKP_MISS_NON_SECURE_INTR:
- When RX look up miss event occurs, hw will assert secure/non-secure
intr based on this bit. Reset_Domain: Secure_Reset. 0 = SECURE_INTR 1 = NON_SECURE_INTR 22:21 0x2 VALIDATE_FRAMES:
- MACSEC Receive Frame Validate control
Reset_Domain: Secure_Reset. 0 = DISABLED :ICV check is disabled. SecTag and ICV fields are removed from the frame before forwarding it to the next module 1 = CHECK :ICV check is done. And the InPktsInValid counter is updated based on ICV check result. 2 = STRICT :ICV check is done. If ICV check fails, the frame is dropped (CRC of the frame is corrupted) and InPktsNotValid counter is updated. 0x1 RX_REPLAY_PROT_EN:
- MACSEC Receive Frame Replay Protection enable control
Reset_Domain: Secure_Reset. 0 = DISABLE :Disable Replay Protection 1 = ENABLE :Enable Replay Protection 0x0 RX_LOOKUP_MISS:
- MACSEC Receive: Select an action for Bypass LookUP tables miss (No
matching entry found in the Bypass LUT). This bit is applicable only for
- Bypass LuT and not SC index LuT
Reset_Domain: Secure_Reset. 0 = DROP :Corrupt the packet on bypass tables lookup miss 1 = BYPASS :Bypass the packet on bypass tables lookup miss 0x0 RX_ENB:
- MACSEC Receive Controller enable bit. Bypasses the MACSEC RX
controller Reset_Domain: Secure_Reset. 0 = DISABLE :Bypasses MACSEC Receive Controller 1 = ENABLE :Enables MACSEC Receive Controller 0x0 TX_LOOKUP_MISS:
- MACSEC Transmit: Select an action for LookUP tables miss (No
matching entry found in both Bypass and SC-Index LUTs). Reset_Domain: Secure_Reset. 0 = DROP :Corrupt the packet on tables lookup miss 1 = BYPASS :Bypass the packet on tables lookup miss

- MACsec Registers
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 TX_ENB:
- MACSEC Transmit Controller enable bit. Bypasses the MACSEC TX
controller Reset_Domain: Secure_Reset. 0 = DISABLE :Disables MACSEC Transmit Controller 1 = ENABLE :Enables MACSEC Transmit Controller
- MACSEC_LUT_CONFIG_0
- Indirect Addressing access: Register controls for programming the LookUP tables
- Offset: 0xd004
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0b0xxx,xx00,xxxx,x000,xxxx,xxxx,xxx0,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 UPDATE:
- LookUP Table Configuration Update control
- SW has to trigger by writing Logic 1 to the UPDATE field after
programming DATA and other config fields.
- Poll for the value to become Logic0 to ensure the operation is
complete. 0 = DONE :Update operation is done or No update operation is initiated 1 = START :Start the Update operation 0x0 CTLR_SEL:
- MACSEC Controller selection (Transmit or Receiver)
0 = TX :MACSEC Transmitter 1 = RX :MACSEC Receiver 0x0 RW:
- Table access direction
0 = READ :Read entries from LookUP Table 1 = WRITE :Write to LookUP Table 18:16 0x0 LUT_SEL:
- LookUP table Selection control
0 = BYPASS 1 = SC_INDX 2 = SC_PARAM 3 = SC_STATE 4 = SA_STATE 4:0 0x0 TABLE_ENTRY_INDEX:
- Table slot Address or Index where an entry would be written

- MACsec Registers
- MACSEC_LUT_DATA_0
- MACSEC LUT Data register
Following register-set holds the data value for a LookUP table. Format of the data resembles the exact table that is to be programmed. This is an array of 7 identical register entries; the register fields below apply to each entry. Full register list is: MACSEC_LUT_DATA_<i>, among which <i> belongs to <0..6>.
- Offset: 0xd008,..,0xd020
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0b0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description

- DATA

- MACSEC_INTERRUPT_SET0_0
This is a write-only register which can be used to set the interrupt status bit. A write to this register causes the bits in INTERRUPT_STATUS0 register to be set if the corresponding bit in write data is 1'b1. Read always returns 'h0.

- MACSEC_CONTROL1_0
- MACSEC Control Register 1
- Offset: 0xe000
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0b0xxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxx0,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,x0x0)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 INT_LPBK_MODE:
- Internal Loopback mode. When this bit is set to ENABLE, MACSEC TX output
lines will be connectd to MACSEC RX input lines internally. It takes 1us for this bit to take effect inside the MACSEC logic. This bit is also used as the loopback
- FIFO flush bit and needs to be deasserted for 2us for the flush operation to
complete. 0 = DISABLE :Disable Loopback 1 = ENABLE :Enable Loopback 0x0 RX_MTU_CHECK_ENB:
- MACSEC Receive Maximum Transmission Unit Check Control bit
0 = DISABLE :Disable MTU check 1 = ENABLE :Enable MTU check 0x0 TX_LUT_PRIORITY:
- MACSEC Transmit SC and Bypass LUTs priority Control
0 = SC :SC Index LUT has the priority over Bypass LUT 1 = BYPASS :Bypass LUT has the priority over SC-Index LUT 0x0 TX_MTU_CHECK_ENB:
- MACSEC Transmit Maximum Transmission Unit Check Control bit
0 = DISABLE :Disable MTU check 1 = ENABLE :Enable MTU check

- MACsec Registers
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
31:16 0x8e NUM_ERR:
- Number of errors connected to this collator. This is passed as a build
time option to the plugin 5:0 0x5 NUM_ERR_SLICES:
- Number of error slices supported by this error collator, does not
include the GlobalSpace and is derived by ceil (NUM_ERR/32). SW shall first read this register to determine the number of slices and read the required number of Error_Status registers .
- MACSEC_ERRCOLLATOR_SWRESET_0
- Offset: 0xf004
- Read/Write: WO
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxx0)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 SWRST: 1'b1 : Issue a SW reset to the Error Collator. This will reset all the registers(Except SCR), counters and logic of the Error Collator. SW can use this bit to flush errors logged into the error collator for ex, after Boot, SC7/8 exit. 1'b0 : Do nothing, reset value. This bit is auto-cleared.
- MACSEC_ERRCOLLATOR_MISSIONERR_TYPE_0
- Offset: 0xf008
- Read/Write: RO
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000005 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xx00,0101)

- MACsec Registers
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
5:0 0x5 CODE:
- This register indicates the fault code of the error line based on the value
of MISSIONERR_INDEX Register.
- This can be used by a fault handling agent to triage an error without
requiring device-specific code.The possible values of this field are: 6'd0 : None 6'd1 : Parity Error on internal data path 6'd2 : ECC SEC Error on internal data path 6'd3 : ECC DED Error on internal data path 6'd4 : Comparator Error 6'd5 : Register Parity Error 6'd6 : Parity Error from on-chip SRAM/Fifo 6'd7 : ECC SEC Error from on-chip SRAM/Fifo 6'd8 : ECC DED Error from on-chip SRAM/Fifo 6'd9 : Clock Monitor Error 6'd10 : Voltage Error 6'd11 : Temperature Error 6'd12 : CRC Error on internal data path 6'd16 : SW Corrected Error 6'd17 : SW Uncorrected Error 6'd18 : SW Generic Error 6'd20 : ECC SED Error on internal data path 6'd21 : ECC SED Error from on-chip SRAM/Fifo 6'd32 : Other HW Corrected Error 6'd33 : Other HW Uncorrected Error
- All other values : Reserved
- MACSEC_ERRCOLLATOR_CURRENT_COUNTER_VALUE_0
- Offset: 0xf00c
- Read/Write: RO
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxx0,0000,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
8:0 0x0 VALUE:
- Provides the current value of the counter corresponding to the error in
MissionErr_Index Register. Default provides the value of error 0 counter.
- Bit[8] is the ovrerflow bit post which the counter saturates and does not
counter further.
- MACSEC_ERRCOLLATOR_MISSIONERR_USERVALUE_0
- Offset: 0xf010
- Read/Write: RO
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N

- MACsec Registers
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0xdead0000 (0b1101,1110,1010,1101,0000,0000,0000,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
31:0 0xdead0000 VALUE:
- Reflects the value on the error_<i>_user when error_<i>_pulse =
MissionError.
- Only the user signals corresponding to the first error_<i>_pulse
only will b elatched.Subsequent values will be dropped.
- The signals will get latched only when
ERRSLICE<n>_MISSIONERR_STATUS is CLEAR. IPs must tie off the unused bits of this signals to 0, if unused.
- MACSEC_ERRCOLLATOR_MISSIONERR_INDEX_0
- Offset: 0xf014
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,0000,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
7:0 0x0 IDX:
- BINARY Encoded. For error number 32, register should be programmed
with value 0x20. Write to this register with Error number will update:
- MISSIONERR_TYPE Register with the Error-Code for the Error.
- CURRENT_COUNTER_VALUE Register with the error's SEC/DED Counter.
- MISSIONERR_USERVALUE with value of the first error_<i>_user signal.
SW can use this to trage the error. number shall update the MISSIONERR_TYPE register with the error code and the Current_Counter_Value register with the value of the errors SEC/DED counter. SW can use this register to triage the error.
- MACSEC_ERRCOLLATOR_CORRECTABLE_THRESHOLD_0
- Offset: 0xf018
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,0000,0000)

- MACsec Registers
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
7:0 0x0 COUNT:
- Threshold value for all SEC Fault Reporting Units connected to this error
collator.
- SEC Errors are logged once the threshold is reached and the overflow bit
is set. 7'b0 : Log SEC error after receiving 1 Error. 7'b1 : Log SEC error after receiving 2 Errors. ... 7'bFF : Log SEC error after receiving 256 Errors.
- MACSEC_ERRCOLLATOR_MISSIONERR_INJECT_UNLOCK_0
- Offset: 0xf01c
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,0000,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
7:0 0x0 VALUE:
- Writes to ERRSLICE_XXX_MISSIONERR_INJECT registers are disabled until
this register is written with a value of 0xE1.
- This is to prevent an inadvertent safety error injection in the safety plugin
due to: 1. A fault on ERRSLICE_XXX_MISSIONERR_INJECT register itself. 2. Erroneous SW.
- The register shall be written with a value of 0x0 to reestablish the lock after
user has completed the error injection testing. 0xE1 : Unlock the MISSIONERR_INJECT Register 0x0 : Lock the MISSIONERR_INJECT Register 0 = LOCK 225 = UNLOCK
- MACSEC_ERRCOLLATOR_ERRSLICE0_MISSIONERR_ENABLE_0

- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: Y
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0xffffffeb (0b1111,1111,1111,1111,1111,1111,111x,1x11)

- MACSEC_ERRCOLLATOR_ERRSLICE0_LATENTERR_STATUS_0

- MACsec Registers
Bits in this register continue to be logged independent of the value of MissionError_Enable register, to avoid silent dropping of errors.

- MACSEC_ERRCOLLATOR_ERRSLICE1_LATENTERR_STATUS_0
SW must write 1 to clear the fields of this register.

- MACsec Registers
Bits in this register continue to be logged independent of the value of LatentError_Enable register, to avoid silent dropping of errors.

- MACSEC_ERRCOLLATOR_ERRSLICE2_LATENTERR_STATUS_0
